function InitGlobals takes nothing returns nothing
endfunction

function Loglevel_getTag takes integer this returns string
	local integer temp = this
	if temp == 0 then
		return "|cffADADADtrace|r"
	elseif temp == 1 then
		return "|cff2685DCdebug|r"
	elseif temp == 2 then
		return "|cffFFCC00info|r"
	elseif temp == 3 then
		return "|cffF47E3Ewarning|r"
	else
		return "|cffFB2700error|r"
	endif
endfunction

function printLog takes player showTo, integer loglvl, string msg returns nothing
	local string compositeMsg
	if Printing_DEBUG_LEVEL <= loglvl then
		set compositeMsg = Loglevel_getTag(loglvl) + " - " + msg
		call DisplayTimedTextToPlayer(showTo, 0., 0., Printing_DEBUG_MSG_DURATION, compositeMsg)
	endif
endfunction

function Log_error takes string msg returns nothing
	call printLog(Player_localPlayer, 4, msg)
endfunction

function compileError takes string msg returns nothing
endfunction

function hashtable_hasBoolean takes hashtable this, integer parentKey, integer childKey returns boolean
	return HaveSavedBoolean(this, parentKey, childKey)
endfunction

function hashtable_hasInt takes hashtable this, integer parentKey, integer childKey returns boolean
	return HaveSavedInteger(this, parentKey, childKey)
endfunction

function hashtable_loadBoolean takes hashtable this, integer parentKey, integer childKey returns boolean
	return LoadBoolean(this, parentKey, childKey)
endfunction

function hashtable_loadInt takes hashtable this, integer parentKey, integer childKey returns integer
	return LoadInteger(this, parentKey, childKey)
endfunction

function hashtable_saveBoolean takes hashtable this, integer parentKey, integer childKey, boolean value returns nothing
	call SaveBoolean(this, parentKey, childKey, value)
endfunction

function hashtable_saveInt takes hashtable this, integer parentKey, integer childKey, integer value returns nothing
	call SaveInteger(this, parentKey, childKey, value)
endfunction

function real_toInt takes real this returns integer
	return R2I(this)
endfunction

function string_getHash takes string this returns integer
	return StringHash(this)
endfunction

function error takes string msg, string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	local integer hash
	local string stacktraceStr
	local integer stacktraceIndex
	local integer stacktraceLimit
	local string stacktraceStr_1
	local integer stacktraceIndex_1
	local integer stacktraceLimit_1
	local string temp
	local string temp_1
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	if MagicFunctions_compiletime then
		call compileError("ERROR: " + msg)
	else
		if  not ErrorHandling_suppressErrorMessages then
			set hash = string_getHash(msg)
			if hashtable_hasInt(ErrorHandling_HT, ErrorHandling_PRIMARY_ERROR_KEY, hash) then
				if hashtable_loadInt(ErrorHandling_HT, ErrorHandling_PRIMARY_ERROR_KEY, hash) + ErrorHandling_MUTE_ERROR_DURATION < GameTimer_currentTime then
					set temp = msg
					set stacktraceStr = ""
					set stacktraceIndex = wurst_stack_depth
					set stacktraceLimit = 0
					loop
						set stacktraceIndex = stacktraceIndex - 1
						set stacktraceLimit = stacktraceLimit + 1
						exitwhen stacktraceLimit > 20
						exitwhen stacktraceIndex < 0
						set stacktraceStr = stacktraceStr + "\n   " + wurst_stack[stacktraceIndex]
					endloop
					call Log_error(temp + stacktraceStr)
					call hashtable_saveInt(ErrorHandling_HT, ErrorHandling_PRIMARY_ERROR_KEY, hash, real_toInt(GameTimer_currentTime))
					call hashtable_saveBoolean(ErrorHandling_HT, ErrorHandling_PRIMARY_ERROR_KEY, hash, false)
				elseif hashtable_hasBoolean(ErrorHandling_HT, ErrorHandling_PRIMARY_ERROR_KEY, hash) then
					if  not hashtable_loadBoolean(ErrorHandling_HT, ErrorHandling_PRIMARY_ERROR_KEY, hash) then
						call Log_error("|cffFF3A29Excessive repeating errors are being omitted")
						call hashtable_saveBoolean(ErrorHandling_HT, ErrorHandling_PRIMARY_ERROR_KEY, hash, true)
					endif
				else
					call Log_error("|cffFF3A29Excessive repeating errors are being omitted")
					call hashtable_saveBoolean(ErrorHandling_HT, ErrorHandling_PRIMARY_ERROR_KEY, hash, true)
				endif
			else
				call hashtable_saveInt(ErrorHandling_HT, ErrorHandling_PRIMARY_ERROR_KEY, hash, real_toInt(GameTimer_currentTime))
				set temp_1 = "Message: " + msg
				set stacktraceStr_1 = ""
				set stacktraceIndex_1 = wurst_stack_depth
				set stacktraceLimit_1 = 0
				loop
					set stacktraceIndex_1 = stacktraceIndex_1 - 1
					set stacktraceLimit_1 = stacktraceLimit_1 + 1
					exitwhen stacktraceLimit_1 > 20
					exitwhen stacktraceIndex_1 < 0
					set stacktraceStr_1 = stacktraceStr_1 + "\n   " + wurst_stack[stacktraceIndex_1]
				endloop
				call Log_error(temp_1 + stacktraceStr_1)
			endif
		endif
		call I2S(1 / 0)
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

function alloc_LLEntry takes string w__wurst_stackPos returns integer
	local integer this
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	if LLEntry_firstFree == 0 then
		if LLEntry_maxIndex < JASS_MAX_ARRAY_SIZE then
			set LLEntry_maxIndex = LLEntry_maxIndex + 1
			set this = LLEntry_maxIndex
			set LLEntry_typeId[this] = 714
		else
			call error("Out of memory: Could not create LLEntry.", "when calling error in LinkedList, line 428")
			set this = 0
		endif
	else
		set LLEntry_firstFree = LLEntry_firstFree - 1
		set this = LLEntry_nextFree[LLEntry_firstFree]
		set LLEntry_typeId[this] = 714
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
	return this
endfunction

		endif
	else
		set LinkedList_firstFree = LinkedList_firstFree - 1

		set LinkedList_typeId[this] = 718
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
	return this
endfunction

function max_2 takes integer numbers_0, integer numbers_1 returns integer
	local integer maxNumber = Integer_INT_MIN
	local integer cond_result
	if numbers_0 > maxNumber then
		set cond_result = numbers_0
	else
		set cond_result = maxNumber
	endif
	set maxNumber = cond_result
	if numbers_1 > maxNumber then
		set cond_result = numbers_1
	else
		set cond_result = maxNumber
	endif
	set maxNumber = cond_result
	return maxNumber
endfunction

	return SubString(this, start, stop)
endfunction

function string_indexOf takes string this, string s returns integer
	local integer len = string_length(s)
	local integer i = 0
	local integer temp = string_length(this) - len
	loop
		exitwhen i > temp
		if string_substring(this, i, i + len) == s then
			return i
		endif
		set i = i + 1
	endloop
	return -1
endfunction

function string_indexOf_820 takes string this, string s, integer startpos returns integer
	local integer i = startpos
	local integer temp = string_length(this) - string_length(s)
	loop
		exitwhen i > temp
		if string_substring(this, i, i + string_length(s)) == s then
			return i
		endif
		set i = i + 1
	endloop
	return -1
endfunction

function string_replace takes string this, string oldSubstring, string newSubstring returns string
	local string s = this
	local integer i
	if string_length(oldSubstring) > 0 then
		set i = string_indexOf(this, oldSubstring)
		loop
			exitwhen  not (i != -1)
			set s = string_substring(s, 0, i) + newSubstring + string_substring(s, i + string_length(oldSubstring), string_length(s))
			set i = string_indexOf_820(s, oldSubstring, i + string_length(newSubstring))
		endloop
	endif
	return s
endfunction

function string_format_1 takes string this, string replacements_0 returns string
	local string result_1 = this
	local integer i = 0
	set result_1 = string_replace(result_1, "{" + int_toString(i) + "}", replacements_0)
	set i = i + 1
	return result_1
endfunction

function buy_attribute takes player p_1, string attributestr, string amountstr, string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	local integer attribute
	local integer attributeCostGold
	local string temp
	local real attributeCostLumber
	local integer askedAmount
	local integer possibleAttributeGold
	local integer possibleAttributeLumber
	local integer possibleAttributeTotal
	local integer givenAttributeTotal
	local integer givenAttributeGold
	local integer givenAttributeLumber
	local unit hero
	local integer temp_1
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set temp = attributestr
	if temp == "str" or temp == "strength" then
		set attribute = 0
		set attributeCostGold = 100
	elseif temp == "agi" or temp == "agility" then
		set attribute = 1
		set attributeCostGold = 100
	elseif temp == "int" or temp == "intelligence" then
		set attribute = 2
		set attributeCostGold = 100
	elseif temp == "lvl" or temp == "level" then
		set attribute = 3
		set attributeCostGold = 20000
	else
		call player_print(p_1, string_format_1("Unknown attribute {0}", attributestr), Constants_message_duration)
		set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
		return
	endif
	set attributeCostLumber = attributeCostGold / Constants_goldToLumber
	if amountstr == "max" then
		set askedAmount = -1
	else
		set askedAmount = string_toInt(amountstr)
	endif
	set possibleAttributeGold = real_toInt(player_getGold(p_1) * 1. / attributeCostGold)
	set possibleAttributeLumber = real_toInt(player_getLumber(p_1) / attributeCostLumber)
	set possibleAttributeTotal = possibleAttributeGold + possibleAttributeLumber
	if possibleAttributeTotal == 0 then
		call player_print(p_1, "Not enough money!", Constants_message_duration)
		if  not Commands_DEBUG_MODE then
			set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
			return
		endif
	endif
	if askedAmount == -1 then
		set givenAttributeTotal = possibleAttributeTotal
	elseif askedAmount <= possibleAttributeTotal then
		set givenAttributeTotal = askedAmount
	else
		call player_print(p_1, "Not enough money!", Constants_message_duration)
		if  not Commands_DEBUG_MODE then
			set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
			return
		endif
		set givenAttributeTotal = askedAmount
	endif
	set hero = unitFromIndex(dispatch_HashMap_HashMap_HashMap_get(HeroSelection_playerHero, playerToIndex(p_1), "when calling get in Commands, line 154"), "when calling unitFromIndex in Commands, line 154")
	if attribute == 3 then
		set givenAttributeTotal = max_2(givenAttributeTotal, Constants_maximum_level - unit_getLevel(hero))
	endif
	set givenAttributeGold = min_2(possibleAttributeGold, givenAttributeTotal)
	set givenAttributeLumber = givenAttributeTotal - givenAttributeGold
	set temp_1 = attribute
	if temp_1 == 0 then
		call unit_addStr(hero, givenAttributeTotal)
	elseif temp_1 == 1 then
		call unit_addAgi(hero, givenAttributeTotal)
	elseif temp_1 == 2 then
		call unit_addInt(hero, givenAttributeTotal)
	else
		call unit_addLevels(hero, givenAttributeTotal, true)
	endif
	call player_subGold(p_1, givenAttributeGold * attributeCostGold)
	call player_subGold(p_1, real_toInt(givenAttributeLumber * attributeCostLumber))
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

function int_clamp takes integer this, integer lowerBound, integer higherBound returns integer
	local integer cond_result
	local integer cond_result_1
	if this <= lowerBound then
		set cond_result_1 = lowerBound
	else
		if this >= higherBound then
			set cond_result = higherBound
		else
			set cond_result = this
		endif
		set cond_result_1 = cond_result
	endif
	return cond_result_1
endfunction

function stringToIndex takes string s, string w__wurst_stackPos returns integer
	local integer hash
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set hash = string_getHash(s)
	loop
		exitwhen  not true
		if dispatch_Table_Table_Table_hasString(TypeCasting_typecastdata, hash, "when calling hasString in TypeCasting, line 32") then
			if dispatch_Table_Table_Table_loadString(TypeCasting_typecastdata, hash, "when calling loadString in TypeCasting, line 33") == s then
				exitwhen true
			endif
		else
			call dispatch_Table_Table_Table_saveString(TypeCasting_typecastdata, hash, s, "when calling saveString in TypeCasting, line 36")
			exitwhen true
		endif
		set hash = hash + 1
	endloop
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
	return hash
endfunction

function string_split takes string this, string splitBy, string w__wurst_stackPos returns integer
	local integer list
	local integer offset
	local string str
	local integer splitIndex
	local string first
	local string second
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set list = new_LinkedList("when calling new_LinkedList in StringUtils, line 91")
	set offset = string_length(splitBy)
	set str = this
	loop
		exitwhen  not true
		set splitIndex = string_indexOf(str, splitBy)
		if splitIndex == -1 then
			call dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_add_1(list, stringToIndex(str, "when calling stringToIndex in StringUtils, line 97"), "when calling add in StringUtils, line 97")
			exitwhen true
		endif
		set first = string_substring(str, 0, splitIndex)
		set second = string_substring(str, splitIndex + offset, string_length(str))
		call dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_add_1(list, stringToIndex(first, "when calling stringToIndex in StringUtils, line 101"), "when calling add in StringUtils, line 101")
		set str = second
	endloop
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
	return list
endfunction

function updateIncome takes player p_1, string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	local integer inc
	local integer iRow
	local integer pTeam
	local integer iTeam
	local integer temp
	local integer team
	local multiboard receiver
	local multiboard receiver_1
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set inc = dispatch_HashMap_HashMap_HashMap_get(IncomeValues_playerIncome, player_getId(p_1), "when calling get in IncomeBoard, line 85")
	set iRow = 1
	set pTeam = player_getTeam(p_1)
	set iTeam = 0
	set temp = pTeam
	loop
		exitwhen iTeam > temp
		set team = Teams_teams[iTeam]
		if  not dispatch_Team_Teams_Team_isEmpty(team, "when calling isEmpty in IncomeBoard, line 90") then
			set iRow = iRow + 1 + dispatch_Team_Teams_Team_playerCount(team, "when calling playerCount in IncomeBoard, line 91")
		endif
		set iTeam = iTeam + 1
	endloop
	set receiver = IncomeBoard_incomeBoard
	call multiboard_setItemValue_717(receiver, iRow, 1, Money_gold[inc])
	set receiver_1 = receiver
	call multiboard_setItemValue_717(receiver_1, iRow, 2, Money_lumber[inc])
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

function handleCommand takes string str, string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	local player p_1
	local integer args
	local string cmd
	local string temp
	local string zoomstr
	local integer zoom
	local string enable
	local string temp_1
	local string whichstr
	local integer amount
	local string temp_2
	local integer inc
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set p_1 = GetTriggerPlayer()
	set args = string_split(string_substring_826(str, 1), " ", "when calling split in Commands, line 46")
	call stringFromIndex(dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_getFirst(args, "when calling getFirst in Commands, line 48"), "when calling stringFromIndex in Commands, line 48")
	set cmd = stringFromIndex(dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_get(args, 0, "when calling get in Commands, line 49"), "when calling stringFromIndex in Commands, line 49")
	set temp = cmd
	if temp == "help" then
		call player_print_780(p_1, "Help:\n" + Commands_help_string)
		if Commands_DEBUG_MODE then
			call player_print_780(p_1, Commands_debug_help_string)
		endif
	elseif temp == "zoom" or temp == "cam" then
		set zoomstr = stringFromIndex(dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_get(args, 1, "when calling get in Commands, line 58"), "when calling stringFromIndex in Commands, line 58")
		set zoom = string_toInt(zoomstr)
		if zoom == 0 then
			set zoom = 100
		endif
		set zoom = int_clamp(zoom, Constants_zoom_minimum, Constants_zoom_maximum)
		call SetCameraFieldForPlayer(p_1, CAMERA_FIELD_TARGET_DISTANCE, 16.5 * zoom, 0.3)
	elseif temp == "buy" then
		call buy_attribute(p_1, stringFromIndex(dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_get(args, 1, "when calling get in Commands, line 67"), "when calling stringFromIndex in Commands, line 67"), stringFromIndex(dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_get(args, 2, "when calling get in Commands, line 67"), "when calling stringFromIndex in Commands, line 67"), "when calling buy_attribute in Commands, line 67")
	elseif temp == "str" or temp == "agi" or temp == "int" or temp == "lvl" then
		call buy_attribute(p_1, cmd, stringFromIndex(dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_get(args, 1, "when calling get in Commands, line 70"), "when calling stringFromIndex in Commands, line 70"), "when calling buy_attribute in Commands, line 70")
	elseif temp == "hlwdbgsecret" then
		set enable = stringFromIndex(dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_get(args, 1, "when calling get in Commands, line 73"), "when calling stringFromIndex in Commands, line 73")
		set temp_1 = enable
		if temp_1 == "on" or temp_1 == "" then
			set Commands_DEBUG_MODE = true
			call player_print(p_1, "Debug mode enabled", Constants_message_duration)
		elseif temp_1 == "off" then
			set Commands_DEBUG_MODE = false
			call player_print(p_1, "Debug mode disabled", Constants_message_duration)
		endif
	elseif temp == "income" then
		set whichstr = stringFromIndex(dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_get(args, 1, "when calling get in Commands, line 83"), "when calling stringFromIndex in Commands, line 83")
		set amount = string_toInt(stringFromIndex(dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_get(args, 2, "when calling get in Commands, line 84"), "when calling stringFromIndex in Commands, line 84"))
		set temp_2 = whichstr
		if temp_2 == "g" then
			set Money_gold[dispatch_HashMap_HashMap_HashMap_get(IncomeValues_playerIncome, player_getId(p_1), "when calling get in Commands, line 87")] = amount
		elseif temp_2 == "l" then
			set Money_lumber[dispatch_HashMap_HashMap_HashMap_get(IncomeValues_playerIncome, player_getId(p_1), "when calling get in Commands, line 89")] = amount
		else
			set inc = dispatch_HashMap_HashMap_HashMap_get(IncomeValues_playerIncome, player_getId(p_1), "when calling get in Commands, line 91")
			set Money_gold[inc] = amount
			set Money_lumber[inc] = amount
		endif
		call updateIncome(p_1, "when calling updateIncome in Commands, line 94")
	else
		call player_print(p_1, string_format_1("Unknown command '{0}'", cmd), Constants_message_duration)
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

function string_startsWith takes string this, string s returns boolean
	local integer len = string_length(this)
	if string_length(s) > len then
		return false
	endif
	return string_substring(this, 0, string_length(s)) == s
endfunction

function toHex takes integer number returns string
	local integer firstpart = number / 16
	local integer secondpart = number - firstpart * 16
	return Colors_hexs[firstpart] + Colors_hexs[secondpart]
endfunction

function color_toColorString takes integer this_red, integer this_green, integer this_blue returns string
	return "|cff" + toHex(this_red) + toHex(this_green) + toHex(this_blue)
endfunction

function player_getColor takes player this returns playercolor
	return GetPlayerColor(this)
endfunction

function player_getName takes player this, boolean removeHash returns string
	local string cond_result
	if removeHash then
		set cond_result = string_substring(GetPlayerName(this), 0, string_indexOf(GetPlayerName(this), "#"))
	else
		set cond_result = GetPlayerName(this)
	endif
	return cond_result
endfunction

function colorA_withoutAlpha takes integer this_red, integer this_green, integer this_blue, integer this_alpha returns integer
	set colorA_withoutAlpha_return_red = this_red
	set colorA_withoutAlpha_return_green = this_green
	set colorA_withoutAlpha_return_blue = this_blue
	return colorA_withoutAlpha_return_red
endfunction

function playercolor_toInt takes playercolor this returns integer
	local integer value = 0
	local integer i = 0
	local integer temp = bj_MAX_PLAYER_SLOTS - 1
	loop
		exitwhen i > temp
		if Playercolor_LOOKUP[i] == this then
			set value = i
			exitwhen true
		endif
		set i = i + 1
	endloop
	return value
endfunction

function playercolor_toColor takes playercolor this returns integer
	local integer cond_result_red
	local integer cond_result_green
	local integer cond_result_blue
	local integer tempIndex
	local integer tuple_temp
	local integer tuple_temp_1
	local integer tuple_temp_2
	local integer tuple_temp_3
	local integer tuple_temp_4
	local integer tuple_temp_5
	if playercolor_toInt(this) <= Colors_MAX_PLAYER_COLORS then
		set tempIndex = playercolor_toInt(this)
		set tuple_temp = Colors_PLAYER_COLORS_red[tempIndex]
		set tuple_temp_1 = Colors_PLAYER_COLORS_green[tempIndex]
		set tuple_temp_2 = Colors_PLAYER_COLORS_blue[tempIndex]
		set cond_result_red = tuple_temp
		set cond_result_green = tuple_temp_1
		set cond_result_blue = tuple_temp_2
	else
		set tuple_temp_3 = colorA_withoutAlpha(Colors_COLOR_BLACK_red, Colors_COLOR_BLACK_green, Colors_COLOR_BLACK_blue, Colors_COLOR_BLACK_alpha)
		set tuple_temp_4 = colorA_withoutAlpha_return_green
		set tuple_temp_5 = colorA_withoutAlpha_return_blue
		set cond_result_red = tuple_temp_3
		set cond_result_green = tuple_temp_4
		set cond_result_blue = tuple_temp_5
	endif
	set playercolor_toColor_return_red = cond_result_red
	set playercolor_toColor_return_green = cond_result_green
	set playercolor_toColor_return_blue = cond_result_blue
	return playercolor_toColor_return_red
endfunction

function player_getNameColored takes player this, boolean removeHash returns string
	return color_toColorString(playercolor_toColor(player_getColor(this)), playercolor_toColor_return_green, playercolor_toColor_return_blue) + player_getName(this, removeHash) + "|r"
endfunction

function LinkedList_remove takes integer this, integer elem, string w__wurst_stackPos returns boolean
	local boolean result_1
	local integer entry
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set result_1 = false
	set entry = LLEntry_next[LinkedList_dummy[this]]
	loop
		exitwhen  not (entry != LinkedList_dummy[this])
		if LLEntry_elem[entry] == elem then
			call dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_removeEntry(this, entry, "when calling removeEntry in LinkedList, line 142")
			set result_1 = true
			exitwhen true
		endif
		set entry = LLEntry_next[entry]
	endloop
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
	return result_1
endfunction

function dispatch_EventListener_ClosureEvents_EventListener_onEvent takes integer this, string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	if EventListener_typeId[this] == 0 then
		if this == 0 then
			call error("Nullpointer exception when calling EventListener.onEvent", "when calling error in ClosureEvents, line 119")
		else
			call error("Called EventListener.onEvent on invalid object.", "when calling error in ClosureEvents, line 119")
		endif
	endif
	if EventListener_typeId[this] <= 658 then
		if EventListener_typeId[this] <= 656 then
			if EventListener_typeId[this] <= 655 then
				call onEvent_add_Commands(this, "when calling onEvent_add_Commands in ClosureEvents, line 119")
			else
				call onEvent_add_HeroRevive(this, "when calling onEvent_add_HeroRevive in ClosureEvents, line 119")
			endif
		elseif EventListener_typeId[this] <= 657 then
			call onEvent_add_HeroSelection(this, "when calling onEvent_add_HeroSelection in ClosureEvents, line 119")
		else
			call onEvent_add_IncomeBoard(this)
		endif
	elseif EventListener_typeId[this] <= 660 then
		if EventListener_typeId[this] <= 659 then
			call onEvent_add_IncomeValues(this, "when calling onEvent_add_IncomeValues in ClosureEvents, line 119")
		else
			call onEvent_add_SpawnKeeps(this)
		endif
	elseif EventListener_typeId[this] <= 661 then
		call onEvent_add_Teams(this, "when calling onEvent_add_Teams in ClosureEvents, line 119")
	else
		call onEvent_add_nullTimer_Players(this, "when calling onEvent_add_nullTimer_Players in ClosureEvents, line 119")
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

	return GetHandleId(this)
endfunction

function eventid_isKeyboardEvent takes eventid this returns boolean
	local integer eventId = handle_getHandleId(this)
	return (eventId >= 261 and eventId <= 268) or eventId == 17
endfunction

function eventid_isMouseEvent takes eventid this returns boolean
	local integer eventId = handle_getHandleId(this)
	return eventId >= 305 and eventId <= 307
endfunction

function eventid_isPlayerunitEvent takes eventid this returns boolean
	local integer eventId = handle_getHandleId(this)
	return (eventId >= 18 and eventId <= 51) or (eventId >= 269 and eventId <= 277) or eventId == 315 or eventId == 308
endfunction

function registerPlayerUnitEvent_811 takes playerunitevent p_1, code filter, code condition, code action returns nothing
	local integer hid = handle_getHandleId(p_1)
	local integer k
	local filterfunc cond_result
	local trigger temp
	local player temp_1
	local playerunitevent temp_2
	if RegisterEvents_t[hid] == null then
		set RegisterEvents_t[hid] = CreateTrigger()
		set k = bj_MAX_PLAYER_SLOTS - 1
		loop
			exitwhen k < 0
			set temp = RegisterEvents_t[hid]
			set temp_1 = Player_players[k]
			set temp_2 = p_1
			if filter != null then
				set cond_result = Filter(filter)
			else
				set cond_result = null
			endif
			call trigger_registerPlayerUnitEvent(temp, temp_1, temp_2, cond_result)
			set k = k - 1
		endloop
	endif
	if condition != null then
		call trigger_addCondition(RegisterEvents_t[hid], Filter(condition))
	endif
	if action != null then
		call trigger_addAction(RegisterEvents_t[hid], action)
	endif
endfunction

function registerPlayerUnitEvent takes playerunitevent p_1, code c returns nothing
	call registerPlayerUnitEvent_811(p_1, null, c, null)
endfunction

function registerEventId takes eventid evnt, string w__wurst_stackPos returns integer
	local integer eventId
	local integer i
	local integer temp
	local trigger receiver
	local trigger receiver_1
	local trigger receiver_2
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set eventId = handle_getHandleId(evnt)
	set ClosureEvents_eventTypeCounter = ClosureEvents_eventTypeCounter + 1
	set ClosureEvents_eventidToIndex[eventId] = ClosureEvents_eventTypeCounter
	if eventid_isPlayerunitEvent(evnt) then
		call registerPlayerUnitEvent(ConvertPlayerUnitEvent(eventId), ref_function_bridge_EventListener_generalEventCallback)
	elseif evnt != EVENT_UNIT_DAMAGED and evnt != EVENT_PLAYER_LEAVE and evnt != ClosureEvents_EVENT_PLAYER_CHAT_FILTER and ( not eventid_isKeyboardEvent(evnt)) and ( not eventid_isMouseEvent(evnt)) then
		call error("registering handleid: " + int_toString(eventId) + " non-playerunitevent. Except EVENT_UNIT_DAMAGED and EVENT_PLAYER_LEAVE these are not supported right now.", "when calling error in ClosureEvents, line 260")
	endif
	if eventid_isMouseEvent(evnt) and ( not EventListener_useMouseEvents) then
		set EventListener_useMouseEvents = true
		set i = 0
		set temp = bj_MAX_PLAYERS - 1
		loop
			exitwhen i > temp
			set receiver = ClosureEvents_keyTrig
			call trigger_registerPlayerEvent(receiver, Player_players[i], EVENT_PLAYER_MOUSE_UP)
			set receiver_1 = receiver
			call trigger_registerPlayerEvent(receiver_1, Player_players[i], EVENT_PLAYER_MOUSE_DOWN)
			set receiver_2 = receiver_1
			call trigger_registerPlayerEvent(receiver_2, Player_players[i], EVENT_PLAYER_MOUSE_MOVE)
			set i = i + 1
		endloop
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
	return ClosureEvents_eventTypeCounter
endfunction

	local integer id

	return id
endfunction

function EventListener_generalEventCallback takes string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	local unit trigUnit
	local integer id
	local integer listener
	local integer nextListener
	local integer listener_1
	local integer nextListener_1
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set trigUnit = GetTriggerUnit()
	set id = eventid_toIntId(GetTriggerEventId(), "when calling toIntId in ClosureEvents, line 184")
	if trigUnit != null and fireEvents(trigUnit) and unit_getIndex(trigUnit) > 0 then
		if EventListener_unitListenersFirsts[unit_getIndex(trigUnit)] != 0 then
			set listener = EventListener_unitListenersFirsts[unit_getIndex(trigUnit)]
			loop
				exitwhen  not (listener != 0)
				set nextListener = EventListener_next[listener]
				if EventListener_eventId[listener] == id then
					call dispatch_EventListener_ClosureEvents_EventListener_onEvent(listener, "when calling onEvent in ClosureEvents, line 192")
				endif
				set listener = nextListener
			endloop
		endif
	endif
	if EventListener_generalListenersFirsts[id] != 0 then
		set listener_1 = EventListener_generalListenersFirsts[id]
		loop
			exitwhen  not (listener_1 != 0)
			set nextListener_1 = EventListener_next[listener_1]
			call dispatch_EventListener_ClosureEvents_EventListener_onEvent(listener_1, "when calling onEvent in ClosureEvents, line 199")
			set listener_1 = nextListener_1
		endloop
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

	endif

endfunction

function unit_toUnitIndex takes unit this, string w__wurst_stackPos returns integer

	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos

			endif

			endif
		elseif OnCastListener_prev[this] != 0 then

		endif
	endif
	set OnCastListener_prev[OnCastListener_next[this]] = OnCastListener_prev[this]

	set OnCastListener_prev[this] = 0
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1

	set EventListener_prev[this] = 0
endfunction

function updateIncomes takes string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	local integer iRow
	local integer iTeam
	local integer team
	local multiboard receiver
	local multiboard receiver_1
	local integer iterator
	local integer id
	local integer pInc
	local multiboard receiver_2
	local multiboard receiver_3
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set iRow = 1
	set iTeam = 0
	loop
		exitwhen iTeam > 3
		set team = Teams_teams[iTeam]
		if  not dispatch_Team_Teams_Team_isEmpty(team, "when calling isEmpty in IncomeBoard, line 72") then
			set receiver = IncomeBoard_incomeBoard
			call multiboard_setItemValue_717(receiver, iRow, 1, Money_gold[IncomeValues_teamIncome[iTeam]])
			set receiver_1 = receiver
			call multiboard_setItemValue_717(receiver_1, iRow, 2, Money_lumber[IncomeValues_teamIncome[iTeam]])
			set iRow = iRow + 1
			set iterator = LinkedList_iterator(Team_playerIds[team], "when calling iterator in IncomeBoard, line 77")
			loop
				exitwhen  not LLIterator_hasNext(iterator)
				set id = LLIterator_next(iterator)
				set pInc = dispatch_HashMap_HashMap_HashMap_get(IncomeValues_playerIncome, id, "when calling get in IncomeBoard, line 78")
				set receiver_2 = IncomeBoard_incomeBoard
				call multiboard_setItemValue_717(receiver_2, iRow, 1, Money_gold[pInc])
				set receiver_3 = receiver_2
				call multiboard_setItemValue_717(receiver_3, iRow, 2, Money_lumber[pInc])
				set iRow = iRow + 1
			endloop
			call LLIterator_close(iterator, "when calling close in IncomeBoard, line 77")
		endif
		set iTeam = iTeam + 1
	endloop
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

function dealloc_HLIterator takes integer obj, string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1

		call error("Double free: object of type HLIterator", "when calling error in HashList, line 157")
	else
		set HLIterator_nextFree[HLIterator_firstFree] = obj
		set HLIterator_firstFree = HLIterator_firstFree + 1
		set HLIterator_typeId[obj] = 0
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

function alloc_HLIterator takes string w__wurst_stackPos returns integer
	local integer this
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	if HLIterator_firstFree == 0 then
		if HLIterator_maxIndex < JASS_MAX_ARRAY_SIZE then
			set HLIterator_maxIndex = HLIterator_maxIndex + 1
			set this = HLIterator_maxIndex
			set HLIterator_typeId[this] = 670
		else
			call error("Out of memory: Could not create HLIterator.", "when calling error in HashList, line 157")
			set this = 0
		endif
	else
		set HLIterator_firstFree = HLIterator_firstFree - 1
		set this = HLIterator_nextFree[HLIterator_firstFree]
		set HLIterator_typeId[this] = 670
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
	return this
endfunction

function incomePeriodic takes string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	local integer i
	local integer iterator
	local integer pId
	local integer income
	local player p_1
	local integer index_temp_29_16
	local integer nLumber
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set i = 0
	loop
		exitwhen i > 3
		call dispatch_Money_Money_Money_reset(IncomeValues_teamIncome[i], "when calling reset in IncomeTimer, line 18")
		set i = i + 1
	endloop
	set iterator = IterableMap_iterator(IncomeValues_playerIncome, "when calling iterator in IncomeTimer, line 21")
	loop
		exitwhen  not HLIterator_hasNext(iterator, "when calling hasNext in IncomeTimer, line 21")
		set pId = HLIterator_next(iterator, "when calling next in IncomeTimer, line 21")
		set income = dispatch_HashMap_HashMap_HashMap_get(IncomeValues_playerIncome, pId, "when calling get in IncomeTimer, line 22")
		set p_1 = Player_players[pId]
		call player_addGold(p_1, Money_gold[income])
		call player_addLumber(p_1, Money_lumber[income])
		set index_temp_29_16 = player_getTeam(p_1)
		set IncomeValues_teamIncome[index_temp_29_16] = Money_op_plus(IncomeValues_teamIncome[index_temp_29_16], income, "when calling op_plus in IncomeTimer, line 29")
		set nLumber = real_toInt(int_toReal(Money_gold[income]) / Constants_goldToLumber)
		set Money_gold[income] = Money_gold[income] - real_toInt(Constants_goldToLumber) * nLumber
		set Money_lumber[income] = Money_lumber[income] + nLumber
		call updateIncome(p_1, "when calling updateIncome in IncomeTimer, line 36")
	endloop
	call HLIterator_close(iterator, "when calling close in IncomeTimer, line 21")
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

	set TimerUtils_freeTimersCount = TimerUtils_freeTimersCount + 1

endfunction

	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	if CallbackSingle_typeId[obj] == 0 then
		call error("Double free: object of type CallbackSingle", "when calling error in ClosureTimers, line 128")
	else
		set CallbackSingle_nextFree[CallbackSingle_firstFree] = obj
		set CallbackSingle_firstFree = CallbackSingle_firstFree + 1
		set CallbackSingle_typeId[obj] = 0
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

function destroyCallbackSingle takes integer this, string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	call CallbackSingle_onDestroy(this, "when calling CallbackSingle_onDestroy in ClosureTimers, line 147")
	call dealloc_CallbackSingle(this, "when calling dealloc_CallbackSingle in ClosureTimers, line 147")
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

function dispatch_CallbackSingle_destroyCallbackSingle takes integer this, string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	if CallbackSingle_typeId[this] == 0 then
		if this == 0 then
			call error("Nullpointer exception when calling CallbackSingle.CallbackSingle", "when calling error in ClosureTimers, line 128")
		else
			call error("Called CallbackSingle.CallbackSingle on invalid object.", "when calling error in ClosureTimers, line 128")
		endif
	endif
	call destroyCallbackSingle(this, "when calling destroyCallbackSingle in ClosureTimers, line 128")
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

function verifyFrameNameLength takes string name, string w__wurst_stackPos returns boolean
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	if string_length(name) > Framehandle_BLZ_FRAMENAME_MAXLENGTH then
		call error("Trying to address frame with exceeding maximum frame name length (" + int_toString(Framehandle_BLZ_FRAMENAME_MAXLENGTH) + ") for: " + name, "when calling error in Framehandle, line 78")
		set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
		return false
	endif
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
	return true
endfunction

	return stackTrace_tempReturn
endfunction

function s2cInit takes nothing returns nothing
	local integer i = 0
	local integer temp = StringUtils_MAX_INDEX
	loop
		exitwhen i > temp
		if string_toUpperCase(StringUtils_c2s[i]) == StringUtils_c2s[i] then
			call StringHash(StringUtils_c2s[i])
		endif
		set i = i + 1
	endloop
endfunction

function onMonsterFinished takes string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	local unit u_1
	local integer team
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set u_1 = GetTriggerUnit()
	if u_1 == OnGoal_u1 then
		set team = 0
	elseif u_1 == OnGoal_u2 then
		set team = 1
	elseif u_1 == OnGoal_u3 then
		set team = 2
	else
		set team = 3
	endif
	call unit_getTypeId(u_1)
	call unit_kill(u_1)
	set Team_lives[Teams_teams[team]] = Team_lives[Teams_teams[team]] - 1
	call updateLives("when calling updateLives in OnGoal, line 30")
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

function bridge_onMonsterFinished takes nothing returns nothing
	set wurst_stack_depth = 0
	call onMonsterFinished("via function reference OnGoal, line 41")
endfunction

function LinkedList_indexOf takes integer this, integer t returns integer
	local integer entry = LLEntry_next[LinkedList_dummy[this]]
	local integer idx = 0
	loop
		exitwhen  not (entry != LinkedList_dummy[this])
		if LLEntry_elem[entry] == t then
			return idx
		endif
		set entry = LLEntry_next[entry]
		set idx = idx + 1
	endloop
	return -1
endfunction

function dispatch_LinkedList_LinkedList_LinkedList_indexOf takes integer this, integer t, string w__wurst_stackPos returns integer
	local integer LinkedList_LinkedList_indexOf_result
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	if LinkedList_typeId[this] == 0 then
		if this == 0 then
			call error("Nullpointer exception when calling LinkedList.indexOf", "when calling error in LinkedList, line 68")
		else
			call error("Called LinkedList.indexOf on invalid object.", "when calling error in LinkedList, line 68")
		endif
	endif
	set LinkedList_LinkedList_indexOf_result = LinkedList_indexOf(this, t)
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
	return LinkedList_LinkedList_indexOf_result
endfunction

endfunction

function onMonsterTrained takes string w__wurst_stackPos returns nothing
	local unit u_1
	local player p_1
	local region r
	local player newOwner
	local integer teamFrom
	local integer i
	local integer temp
	set wurst_stack[wurst_stack_depth] = w__wurst_stackPos
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth + 1
	set u_1 = GetEnteringUnit()
	set p_1 = unit_getOwner(u_1)
	set r = GetTriggeringRegion()
	if r == GameRegions_region_T1Keeps then
		set newOwner = Player_players[19]
		set teamFrom = 0
	elseif r == GameRegions_region_T2Keeps then
		set newOwner = Player_players[20]
		set teamFrom = 1
	elseif r == GameRegions_region_T3Keeps then
		set newOwner = Player_players[21]
		set teamFrom = 2
	elseif r == GameRegions_region_T4Keeps then
		set newOwner = Player_players[22]
		set teamFrom = 3
	else
		call Log_error("onMonsterTrained() was triggered by an unknown region")
		set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
		return
	endif
	call unit_setOwner(u_1, newOwner, true)
	set i = GetRandomInt(0, 7)
	loop
		exitwhen  not (i == 2 * teamFrom or i == 2 * teamFrom + 1)
		set i = GetRandomInt(0, 7)
	endloop
	set temp = i
	if temp == 0 or temp == 1 then
		call unit_setPos(u_1, rect_randomPoint(GameRegions_rects_T1_Spawn[ModuloInteger(i, 2)]), rect_randomPoint_return_y)
	elseif temp == 2 or temp == 3 then
		call unit_setPos(u_1, rect_randomPoint(GameRegions_rects_T2_Spawn[ModuloInteger(i, 2)]), rect_randomPoint_return_y)
	elseif temp == 4 or temp == 5 then
		call unit_setPos(u_1, rect_randomPoint(GameRegions_rects_T3_Spawn[ModuloInteger(i, 2)]), rect_randomPoint_return_y)
	elseif temp == 6 or temp == 7 then
		call unit_setPos(u_1, rect_randomPoint(GameRegions_rects_T4_Spawn[ModuloInteger(i, 2)]), rect_randomPoint_return_y)
	endif
	call dispatch_IterableMap_HashMap_IterableMap_put(IncomeValues_playerIncome, player_getId(p_1), Money_op_plus(dispatch_HashMap_HashMap_HashMap_get(IncomeValues_playerIncome, player_getId(p_1), "when calling get in MoveToSpawn, line 48"), monsterIncome(u_1, "when calling monsterIncome in MoveToSpawn, line 48"), "when calling op_plus in MoveToSpawn, line 48"), "when calling put in MoveToSpawn, line 48")
	set wurst_stack_depth = wurst_stack_depth - 1
endfunction

	call onMonsterTrained("via function reference MoveToSpawn, line 57")

function prepareUnit takes unit u_1 returns nothing
	local unit receiver = u_1
	local unit receiver_1
	call unit_addAbility(receiver, OnUnitEnterLeave_ABILITY_ID)
	set receiver_1 = receiver
	call unit_makeAbilityPermanent(receiver_1, OnUnitEnterLeave_ABILITY_ID, true)
	call pushUnit(u_1)
	call trigger_evaluate(OnUnitEnterLeave_eventTrigger)
	call popUnit()
endfunction

endfunction

endfunction

function code__addAction_Money takes nothing returns nothing
	local player p_1
	local integer nLumber
	call print("Gold more")
	set p_1 = GetTriggerPlayer()
	set nLumber = real_toInt((player_getGold(p_1) - Constants_goldToLumber) / Constants_goldToLumber)
	call player_subGold(p_1, nLumber * real_toInt(Constants_goldToLumber))
	call player_addLumber(p_1, nLumber)
endfunction

function code__addAction_Money_461 takes nothing returns nothing
	local player p_1 = GetTriggerPlayer()
	call print("Lumber: " + int_toString(player_getLumber(p_1)))
	if player_getLumber(p_1) >= 1 then
		call player_addGold(p_1, real_toInt(Constants_goldToLumber))
		call player_addLumber(p_1, -1)
	endif
endfunction

function code__registerPlayerUnitEvent_nullTimer_OnUnitEnterLeave takes nothing returns nothing
	local unit leavingUnit = GetTriggerUnit()
	if unit_getAbilityLevel(leavingUnit, OnUnitEnterLeave_ABILITY_ID) == 0 and GetIssuedOrderId() == OrderIds_undefend then
		call pushUnit(leavingUnit)
		call trigger_execute(OnUnitEnterLeave_eventTrigger)
		call popUnit()
	endif
endfunction

function initPows takes nothing returns nothing
	local integer allPows
	local integer i
	local integer temp
	local integer i_1
	local integer temp_1
	set BitSet_pows[0] = 1
	set allPows = 1
	set i = 1
	set temp = BitSet_BITSET_SIZE - 1
	loop
		exitwhen i > temp
		set BitSet_pows[i] = BitSet_pows[i - 1] * 2
		set allPows = int_bitOr(allPows, BitSet_pows[i])
		set i = i + 1
	endloop
	set i_1 = 0
	set temp_1 = BitSet_BITSET_SIZE - 1
	loop
		exitwhen i_1 > temp_1
		call int_bitXor(allPows, BitSet_pows[i_1])
		set i_1 = i_1 + 1
	endloop
endfunction

function init_MagicFunctions takes nothing returns boolean
	set MagicFunctions_compiletime = false
	return true
endfunction

function vec2_op_mult takes real this_x, real this_y, real factor returns real
	set vec2_op_mult_return_x = this_x * factor
	set vec2_op_mult_return_y = this_y * factor
	return vec2_op_mult_return_x
endfunction

function vec2_op_plus takes real this_x, real this_y, real v_x, real v_y returns real
	set vec2_op_plus_return_x = this_x + v_x
	set vec2_op_plus_return_y = this_y + v_y
	return vec2_op_plus_return_x
endfunction

function initMapBounds takes nothing returns nothing
	local rect cond_result
	local region receiver
	local rect cond_result_1
	local region receiver_1
	local real tuple_temp
	local real tuple_temp_1
	local real tuple_temp_2
	local real tuple_temp_3
	local real tuple_temp_4
	local real tuple_temp_5
	local real tuple_temp_6
	local real tuple_temp_7
	if MagicFunctions_compiletime then
		set cond_result = Rect(-1024., -1024., 1024., 1024.)
	else
		set cond_result = GetPlayableMapRect()
	endif
	set MapBounds_playableMapRect = cond_result
	set receiver = CreateRegion()
	call region_addRect(receiver, MapBounds_playableMapRect)
	if MagicFunctions_compiletime then
		set cond_result_1 = Rect(-1536., -1536., 1536., 1536.)
	else
		set cond_result_1 = GetWorldBounds()
	endif
	set MapBounds_boundRect = cond_result_1
	set receiver_1 = CreateRegion()
	call region_addRect(receiver_1, MapBounds_boundRect)
	set MapBounds_boundRegion = receiver_1
	set tuple_temp = rect_getMinX(MapBounds_playableMapRect)
	set tuple_temp_1 = rect_getMinY(MapBounds_playableMapRect)
	set MapBounds_playableMin_x = tuple_temp
	set MapBounds_playableMin_y = tuple_temp_1
	set tuple_temp_2 = rect_getMaxX(MapBounds_playableMapRect)
	set tuple_temp_3 = rect_getMaxY(MapBounds_playableMapRect)
	set MapBounds_playableMax_x = tuple_temp_2
	set MapBounds_playableMax_y = tuple_temp_3
	set tuple_temp_4 = rect_getMinX(MapBounds_boundRect)
	set tuple_temp_5 = rect_getMinY(MapBounds_boundRect)
	set MapBounds_boundMin_x = tuple_temp_4
	set MapBounds_boundMin_y = tuple_temp_5
	set tuple_temp_6 = rect_getMaxX(MapBounds_boundRect)
	set tuple_temp_7 = rect_getMaxY(MapBounds_boundRect)
	set MapBounds_boundMax_x = tuple_temp_6
	set MapBounds_boundMax_y = tuple_temp_7
	call vec2_op_mult(vec2_op_plus(MapBounds_playableMin_x, MapBounds_playableMin_y, MapBounds_playableMax_x, MapBounds_playableMax_y), vec2_op_plus_return_y, .5)
	call vec2_op_mult(vec2_op_plus(MapBounds_boundMin_x, MapBounds_boundMin_y, MapBounds_boundMax_x, MapBounds_boundMax_y), vec2_op_plus_return_y, .5)
endfunction

function init_MapBounds takes nothing returns boolean
	call initMapBounds()
	return true
endfunction

	return true

function isTeamMonster takes nothing returns boolean
	local unit u_1 = GetEnteringUnit()
	return ( not unit_isType(u_1, UNIT_TYPE_HERO)) and unit_isType(u_1, UNIT_TYPE_SUMMONED) and player_getController(unit_getOwner(u_1)) == MAP_CONTROL_COMPUTER
endfunction

function isUserMonster takes nothing returns boolean
	local unit u_1 = GetEnteringUnit()
	return ( not unit_isType(u_1, UNIT_TYPE_HERO)) and unit_isType(u_1, UNIT_TYPE_SUMMONED) and player_getController(unit_getOwner(u_1)) == MAP_CONTROL_USER
endfunction

function unit_issuePointOrderById takes unit this, integer id, real target_x, real target_y returns boolean
	return IssuePointOrderById(this, id, target_x, target_y)
endfunction

function onMonsterIGoal takes nothing returns nothing
	local unit u_1 = GetEnteringUnit()
	local region reg = GetTriggeringRegion()
	local real goalPosition_x
	local real goalPosition_y
	local real tuple_temp
	local real tuple_temp_1
	local real tuple_temp_2
	local real tuple_temp_3
	local real tuple_temp_4
	local real tuple_temp_5
	local real tuple_temp_6
	local real tuple_temp_7
	if reg == GameRegions_region_T1_IGoal then
		set tuple_temp = rect_getCenter(gg_rct_T1Goal)
		set tuple_temp_1 = rect_getCenter_return_y
		set goalPosition_x = tuple_temp
		set goalPosition_y = tuple_temp_1
	elseif reg == GameRegions_region_T2_IGoal then
		set tuple_temp_2 = rect_getCenter(gg_rct_T2Goal)
		set tuple_temp_3 = rect_getCenter_return_y
		set goalPosition_x = tuple_temp_2
		set goalPosition_y = tuple_temp_3
	elseif reg == GameRegions_region_T3_IGoal then
		set tuple_temp_4 = rect_getCenter(gg_rct_T3Goal)
		set tuple_temp_5 = rect_getCenter_return_y
		set goalPosition_x = tuple_temp_4
		set goalPosition_y = tuple_temp_5
	else
		set tuple_temp_6 = rect_getCenter(gg_rct_T4Goal)
		set tuple_temp_7 = rect_getCenter_return_y
		set goalPosition_x = tuple_temp_6
		set goalPosition_y = tuple_temp_7
	endif
	call unit_issuePointOrderById(u_1, OrderIds_patrol, goalPosition_x, goalPosition_y)
endfunction

function onMonsterSpawned takes nothing returns nothing
	local unit u_1 = GetEnteringUnit()
	local real y
	local real temp_tuple_y
	local region reg
	local real goalX
	local real tuple_temp
	call unit_getPos(u_1)
	set tuple_temp = unit_getPos_return_y
	set temp_tuple_y = tuple_temp
	set y = temp_tuple_y
	set reg = GetTriggeringRegion()
	if reg == GameRegions_region_T1_Spawn then
		set goalX = rect_getMaxX(gg_rct_T1IGoal)
	elseif reg == GameRegions_region_T2_Spawn then
		set goalX = rect_getMaxX(gg_rct_T2IGoal)
	elseif reg == GameRegions_region_T3_Spawn then
		set goalX = rect_getMaxX(gg_rct_T3IGoal)
	else
		set goalX = rect_getMaxX(gg_rct_T4IGoal)
	endif
	call unit_issuePointOrderById(u_1, OrderIds_patrol, goalX, y)
endfunction

function main takes nothing returns nothing
	local trigger initTrig
	call initGlobals()
	call initCompiletimeState()
	call SetCameraBounds(( - 5376.0) + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_LEFT), ( - 9728.0) + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_BOTTOM), 5376.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_RIGHT), 9216.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_TOP), ( - 5376.0) + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_LEFT), 9216.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_TOP), 5376.0 - GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_RIGHT), ( - 9728.0) + GetCameraMargin(CAMERA_MARGIN_BOTTOM))
	call SetDayNightModels("Environment\\DNC\\DNCLordaeron\\DNCLordaeronTerrain\\DNCLordaeronTerrain.mdl", "Environment\\DNC\\DNCLordaeron\\DNCLordaeronUnit\\DNCLordaeronUnit.mdl")
	call NewSoundEnvironment("Default")
	call SetAmbientDaySound("CityScapeDay")
	call SetAmbientNightSound("CityScapeNight")
	call SetMapMusic("Music", true, 0)
	call CreateRegions()
	call CreateAllUnits()

function InitCustomPlayerSlots takes nothing returns nothing
	call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(0), 0)
	call SetPlayerColor(Player(0), ConvertPlayerColor(0))
	call SetPlayerRacePreference(Player(0), RACE_PREF_NIGHTELF)

	call SetPlayerController(Player(0), MAP_CONTROL_USER)
	call SetPlayerStartLocation(Player(1), 1)
